(function(){
  function loadSwiper(callback) {
    if (window.Swiper) {
      callback();
    } else {
      var s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/swiper@11/swiper-bundle.min.js';
      s.async = true;
      s.onload = callback;
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    }
  }

  loadSwiper(function() {
    new Swiper(document.querySelector('.is-benefits'), {
      slideClass:   'swiper-slide',
      wrapperClass: 'swiper-wrapper',
      loop:         true,
      autoHeight:   true,
      scrollbar:    { el: '.benefits-scrollbar' },
      navigation:   {
        nextEl: '.benefits-next',
        prevEl: '.benefits-prev'
      },
      breakpoints:  {
        992: { slidesPerView: 2.2, spaceBetween: 24 },
        768: { slidesPerView: 2, spaceBetween: 16 },
        320: { slidesPerView: 1, spaceBetween: 8 }
      }
    });
  });
})();

(function(){
  function loadSwiper(callback) {
    if (window.Swiper) {
      callback();
    } else {
      var s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/swiper@11/swiper-bundle.min.js';
      s.async = true;
      s.onload = callback;
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    }
  }

  loadSwiper(function() {
    new Swiper(document.querySelector('.is-testimonial'), {
      slideClass:   'swiper-slide',
      wrapperClass: 'swiper-wrapper',
      loop:         true,
      autoHeight:   true,
      scrollbar:    { el: '.testimonial-scrollbar' },
      navigation:   {
        nextEl: '.testimonial-next',
        prevEl: '.testimonial-prev'
      },
      breakpoints:  {
        992: { slidesPerView: 2, spaceBetween: 32 },
        768: { slidesPerView: 1, spaceBetween: 24 },
        320: { slidesPerView: 1, spaceBetween: 12 }
      }
    });
  });

<script>
  $(function () {
    if ($(window).width() > 767) {
      $('[tab-function="autoplay"]').each(function () {
        var $tabsMenu = $(this);
        
        // 🔁 Обновляем иконки при загрузке
$tabsMenu.find('.big-tabs_menu-item').each(function () {
  const isActive = $(this).hasClass('cc-active');
  const icon = $(this).find('.big-tabs_menu-icon.active');

  if (icon.length) {
    icon.toggleClass('is-visible', isActive);
  }
});
        $tabsMenu.find('.big-tabs_menu-item').on('click', function () {
          // Обновляем активный таб
          $tabsMenu.find('.big-tabs_menu-item').removeClass('cc-active');
          $(this).addClass('cc-active');

          // ▶️ Управляем видео + иконками
          $tabsMenu.find('.big-tabs_menu-item').each(function () {
            const isActive = $(this).hasClass('cc-active');
            const videos = $(this).find('video');
            const icon = $(this).find('.big-tabs_menu-icon.active');

            // Видео
            videos.each(function () {
              if (isActive) {
                this.play().catch(() => {});
              } else {
                this.pause();
              }
            });

            // Иконка
            if (icon.length) {
  icon.toggleClass('is-visible', isActive);
}
          });
        });
      });
    }
  });
</script>
